namespace = spirits

##############################################################
# 000-099 = debug/misc
# 100-150 = nature spirits
# 150-200 = undead spirits
# 200-299 = ancestor spirits
# 300-399 = spirit beasts
# 400-499 = temple events
# 500-599 = temple quest events
# 600-699 = temple corruption/misc LHP
# 700-899 = rending events
# 900-999 = country-specific events
# Temple Provinces: 4380, 4384, 4397, 4411, 4417, 4420, 4438, 4450, 4465, 4469, 4488, 4499, 4510, 4527, 4546d, 4565, 4570 4580, 4630d, 4633d, 4764, 4811, 4839d, 4859, 4871, 4925, 4930, 4941d, 4949, 4951, 4955d, 4964, 4979, 4618d
# If you want to downgrade a temple province, use the scripted effect 'downgrade_temple_wards = yes' in the temple province scope AFTER (very important!) downgrading the temple province modifier itself, same for upgrading
##############################################################

province_event = {	#Handler event, determines which spirit event the country gets
	id = spirits.000
	title = spirits.000.t
	desc = spirits.000.d
	picture = MIRACLE_MONK_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		always = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		owner = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = spirit_event_cooldown
				duration = 730
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Corrupted Temple Redirect

country_event = {	#Startup event to give out hidden wards modifiers

	title = spirits.000.t
	desc = spirits.000.d
	picture = MIRACLE_MONK_eventPicture

		always = yes
	}

province_event = {	#Hidden event to determine if temple is damaged by siege
	id = spirits.002
	title = spirits.002.t
	desc = spirits.002.d
	picture = SIEGE_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_province_modifier = temple_complex
			has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
		}
	}
	
	hidden = yes
	
	option = {
		name = spirits.002.a
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { has_province_modifier = temple_complex }
		random_list = {
			75 = {
			}
			25 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.2
					controller = { NOT = { mil_tech = 7 } }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					controller = {
						mil_tech = 7
						NOT = { mil_tech = 13 }
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					controller = {
						mil_tech = 16
						NOT = { mil_tech = 22 }
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					controller = {
						mil_tech = 22
						NOT = { mil_tech = 25 }
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					controller = {
						mil_tech = 25
						NOT = { mil_tech = 32 }
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 3
					controller = {
						mil_tech = 32
					}
				}
				ROOT = { province_event = { id = spirits.003 } }
			}
		}
	}

		}

province_event = {	#Temple damaged by siege
	id = spirits.003
	title = spirits.003.t
	desc = spirits.003.d
	picture = SIEGE_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = spirits.003.a
		goto = ROOT
		add_devastation = 15
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = temple_complex }
			remove_province_modifier = temple_complex
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = damaged_temple_complex
				duration = -1
			}
			downgrade_temple_wards = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex }
			remove_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = derelict_temple_complex
				duration = -1
			}
			downgrade_temple_wards = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				province_id = 4925
			}
			add_great_project_tier = {
			    type = temple_of_undying_flame
			    tier = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {	#Temple restored
	id = spirits.004
	title = spirits.004.t
	desc = spirits.004.d
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = temple_restoration_efforts
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_province_modifier = temple_restoration_efforts
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
					subtract_variable = {
						which = NumTemplesRestoring
						value = 1
					}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = temple_complex
					duration = -1
				}
				upgrade_temple_wards = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = temple_complex
					duration = -1
				}
				upgrade_temple_wards = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = spirits.004.a
		goto = ROOT
		custom_tooltip = temple_restored_tt
	}
}

country_event = { # reset menu
	id = spirits.018
	title = spirits.018.title
	desc = spirits.018.desc
	picture = EMPTY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

		always = yes
	}

		name = spirits.018.a
		clr_country_flag = temple_restoration_menu_reset
		country_event = { id = spirits.005 }
	}

province_event = { #Cleanup event to clear restoration/corruption/temple quest flags if a province being restored/temple being explored is lost
	id = spirits.006
	title = spirits.006.t
	desc = spirits.006.d
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_province_modifier = temple_restoration_efforts
			has_province_modifier = rite_of_corruption
			has_province_modifier = azjakuma_rite_of_corruption
			has_province_flag = temple_being_quested
			has_province_flag = temple_heart_trail
			has_province_modifier = temple_heart_discovered
			has_province_modifier = rite_of_purification
		}
	}
	
	hidden = yes
	
	option = {
		name = spirits.006.a
		clr_province_flag = temple_heart_trail
		remove_province_modifier = temple_heart_discovered
		if = { limit = { has_province_flag = temple_being_quested }
			clr_province_flag = temple_being_quested
			FROM = {
				end_temple_quest = yes
				temple_quest_cash_out = yes
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { OR = { has_province_modifier = rite_of_corruption has_province_modifier = azjakuma_rite_of_corruption } }
			remove_province_modifier = rite_of_corruption
			remove_province_modifier = azjakuma_rite_of_corruption
		}
		if = { limit = { has_province_modifier = temple_restoration_efforts }
			remove_province_modifier = temple_restoration_efforts
		}
		if = { limit = { has_province_modifier = rite_of_purification }
			remove_province_modifier = rite_of_purification
		}
	}
}

province_event = {	#Temple Purified
	id = spirits.008
	title = spirits.008.t
	desc = spirits.008.d
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = rite_of_purification
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = was_temple_complex }
			hidden_effect = {
				purify_temple_wards = yes
				remove_province_triggered_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
				add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = temple_complex duration = -1 }
			}
			clr_province_flag = was_temple_complex
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = was_damaged_temple_complex }
			hidden_effect = {
				purify_temple_wards = yes
				remove_province_triggered_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
				add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = damaged_temple_complex duration = -1 }
			}
			clr_province_flag = was_damaged_temple_complex
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = was_derelict_temple_complex }
			hidden_effect = {
				purify_temple_wards = yes
				remove_province_triggered_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
				add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = derelict_temple_complex duration = -1 }
			}
			clr_province_flag = was_derelict_temple_complex
		}
		remove_province_modifier = rite_of_purification
	}
	
	option = {
		name = spirits.008.a
		goto = ROOT
		custom_tooltip = temple_purified_tt
	}
}

province_event = { #Continue Temple Plundering
	id = spirits.010
	title = spirits.010.t
	desc = spirits.010.d
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = temple_being_plundered
	}
	
	option = {	#Continue Plundering
        name = spirits.010.a
        ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				religion = high_philosophy
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				has_estate = estate_artificers
				OR = { 
					artifice_has_points_10 = yes
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_drills
				}
			}
		}

		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_drills } }
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_drills
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {	#End Plundering
        name = spirits.010.b
        ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				owner = { religion_group = halessi }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				owner = { religion_group = raheni }
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				has_estate = estate_artificers
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_province_flag = temple_being_plundered
			clr_province_flag = permanent_precursor_relics
			REB = {
				subtract_variable = {
					which = num_precursor_relics
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		set_from_saved_trade_goods = yes
	}
	
	option = {	#Don't have Artificers, automatically ends plundering
        name = spirits.010.c
        ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		trigger = { NOT = { owner = { has_estate = estate_artificers } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_province_flag = temple_being_plundered
			clr_province_flag = permanent_precursor_relics
			REB = {
				subtract_variable = {
					which = num_precursor_relics
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		set_from_saved_trade_goods = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Temple Plundering Heart Discovery Pulse
	id = spirits.011
	title = spirits.010.t
	desc = spirits.010.d
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_drills
		any_owned_province = {
			has_province_flag = temple_being_plundered
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex }
		}
	}
	
	option = {	#Nothing
        name = spirits.010.a
        ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
	}
	
	option = {	#Heart Discovery
        name = spirits.010.a
        ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = temple_being_plundered
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = temple_heart_discovered
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
			remove_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail
			save_event_target_as = temple_heart_discovery_target
			province_event = { id = spirits.012 }
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #Heart Discovery
	id = spirits.012
	title = spirits.012.t
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT
	
	desc = {	#Plundering Temple
		trigger = {
			has_province_flag = temple_being_plundered
		}
		desc = spirits.012.da
	}
	
	desc = {	#Questing Temple
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_province_flag = temple_being_plundered }
		}
		desc = spirits.012.db
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	option = {	#Give it to artificers to study
        name = spirits.012.a
		trigger = { owner = { has_estate = estate_artificers } }
		owner = {
			add_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
				estate = estate_artificers
				desc = EST_VAL_GAVE_HEART_TO_ARTIFICERS_LOY
				loyalty = 10
				duration = 7300
			}
			mission_reward_artifice_points_2 = yes
		}
		ruin_temple = yes
        ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				owner = {
					estate_influence = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						influence = 30
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				owner = {
					estate_influence = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						influence = 40
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				owner = {
					estate_influence = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						influence = 50
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {	#Let the mages use it
        name = spirits.012.b
		trigger = { owner = { has_estate = estate_mages } }
		owner = {
			add_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
				estate = estate_mages
				desc = EST_VAL_GAVE_HEART_TO_MAGES_LOY
				loyalty = 10
				duration = 7300
			}
			add_estate_influence_modifier = {	#Empowers the spells they can cast for a bit
				estate = estate_mages
				desc = EST_VAL_GAVE_HEART_TO_MAGES
				influence = 33
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		ruin_temple = yes
        ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				owner = {
					estate_influence = {
						estate = estate_mages
						influence = 30
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				owner = {
					estate_influence = {
						estate = estate_mages
						influence = 40
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				owner = {
					estate_influence = {
						estate = estate_mages
						influence = 50
					}
				}

	desc = spirits.013.d

		is_year = 1580	#Canonical date for the proliferation of Black Damestear creation is late 16th century
		2334 = { NOT = { has_province_flag = inquiry_into_temple_wards_published } }
		OR = {
			has_estate = estate_artificers
			has_estate = estate_dragon_command
			AND = {
				is_year = 1610
				4871 = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					has_province_modifier = gnomish_institute_gommo
				}
			}
		}
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = gnomish_institute_gommo
				has_province_flag = special_gnomish_quarter_gommo
			}
			continent = asia
			NOT = { superregion = forbidden_lands_superregion }
		}
	}
	
	hidden = yes

				factor = 0

			}

					has_province_flag = special_gnomish_quarter_gommo
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = temple_inquiry_institute_target
		}
		country_event = { id = spirits.014 } #Inquiry into Wards
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_artificers
					influence = 30
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_artificers
					influence = 40
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_artificers
					influence = 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_artificers
					influence = 60
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_artificers
					influence = 70
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				influence = 70
			}
		}

			has_country_flag = spirits_funded_korashi_drill_research
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_year = 1700
		}

#ngoho
country_event = {
	id = spirits.170
	title = spirits.170.t
	desc = spirits.170.d
	picture = HIGH_TEMPLE_IN_DISTANCE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spirits.170.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = honsai_ghostemperor_alive }
			custom_tooltip = life_force_tiny_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = honsai_lifespan
					value = 1
				}	
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				3 = {
					add_ruler_modifier = {
						name = spirits_long_life
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				1 = {
					make_ruler_immortal = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = spirits.298
	title = spirits.298.t
	desc = spirits.298.d
	picture = MIRACLE_MONK_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes 

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = rending_active
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = rending_corrupt_flag
			has_country_flag = rending_appease_flag
			has_country_flag = rending_ward_flag
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.298.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				continent = asia
				NOT = { superregion = forbidden_lands_superregion }
				has_province_modifier = rending_unhindered_spirits
			}
			province_event = {
				id = spirits.299
				days = 180
				random = 180
			}
		}
	}
}

#sword spirit
country_event = {
	id = spirits.208
	title = spirits.208.t
	desc = spirits.208.d
	picture = MIRACLE_MONK_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {	#I shall face it
		name = spirits.208.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				mil = 6
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					kill_ruler = yes
				}
				50 = {
					add_prestige_excess_to_splendour_effect = { VAL = 50 }
					increase_ruler_adm_effect = yes
					increase_ruler_dip_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				99 = {
					kill_ruler = yes
				}
				1 = {
					add_prestige_excess_to_splendour_effect = { VAL = 50 }
					increase_ruler_adm_effect = yes
					increase_ruler_dip_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#my advisor will fight
		name = spirits.208.b
		trigger = {
			court_mage = 1
		}
		highlight = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		random_list = {
			90 = {
				kill_advisor_by_category_effect = {
					ADM = yes
				}
			}
			10 = {
				add_prestige_excess_to_splendour_effect = { VAL = 25 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#go general
		name = spirits.208.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = {
			has_leader_with = {
				shock = 5
				general = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		random_list = {
			70 = {
				kill_leader = {
					type = general
				}
			}
			30 = {
				add_prestige_excess_to_splendour_effect = { VAL = 25 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#send all the fucking men you can find
		name = spirits.208.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_stability = -1
		add_yearly_manpower = -1
	}
}

			allow_new_heir = no
		}

		}

			factor = 1

		hidden_effect = {

							trade_goods = sugar

							trade_goods = tropical_wood

						add_devastation = 20
					}
					random = {
						chance = 50
						add_base_production = -1
						add_devastation = 20
					}
				}
			}
		}

#shady path shady hand
country_event = {
	id = spirits.223
	title = spirits.223.t
	desc = spirits.223.d
	picture = LOOMING_DEATH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					culture = horned_ogre
					religion = lefthand_path
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_country = {
				tag = Y01
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.223.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_ruler_religion = lefthand_path
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.223.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {
						religion = lefthand_path
						culture = horned_ogre
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = spirits_lefthand_path_tt
			tooltip = {
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = { OR = { religion = lefthand_path culture = horned_ogre } }
					add_unrest = 5
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { OR = { religion = lefthand_path culture = horned_ogre } }
					add_unrest = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = spirits.230
	title = spirits.230.t
	desc = spirits.230.d
	picture = LOOMING_DEATH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			heir_adm = 2
			heir_dip = 2
			heir_mil = 2
		}
		heir_age = 15
		has_female_heir = no
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.230.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		exile_heir_as = spirits_replacedheir
		define_heir = {
			name = spirits_replacedheir
			adm = 2
			dip = 2
			mil = 5
			age = 15
		}
		set_heir_mage_effect = yes
		set_heir_flag = spirit_corrupt_heir
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spirits.231
				days = 180
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {	#Handler event, determines which TEMPLE event the country gets
	id = spirits.400
	title = spirits.400.t
	desc = spirits.400.d
	picture = MIRACLE_MONK_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex }
	}
	
	option = {	#Temple Event
		name = spirits.400.a
		
		random_list = {
			200 = {
				trigger = {
					religion = high_philosophy
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
					}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = temple_restoration_efforts }
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.401 } #Philosophers Demand Restoration of Temples
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					religion = high_philosophy
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.402 } #Riot at the Temple Complex
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					has_province_modifier = temple_complex
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.403 } #Temple Falls into Disrepair
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.404 } #Earthquake Strikes Temple Complex
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.405 } #Surge of pilgrims
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.406 } #fantastic feast
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.407 } #scholars gather
			}
			5 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.408 } #loaded with qi
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
						religion = owner
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.409 } #scholars quarrel
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.410 } #growing attraction
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.411 } #growing piety
			}
			5 = {
				trigger = {
					has_province_modifier = temple_complex
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.412 } #center of trade and faith
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					has_any_ogre_pop_trigger = yes
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.413 } #local oni damage a temple
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.415 } #sponsor treasure hunters
			}
			10 = {
				province_event = { id = spirits.416 } #monkey mural
			}
			10 = {
				province_event = { id = spirits.417 } #moon mural
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							has_estate = estate_middlecastes
							has_estate = estate_burghers
						}
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.418 } #merchants argue in the temple
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.419 } #moon cult
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.420 } #horny cult
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						controlled_by = owner
						owner = {
							any_owned_province = {
								has_province_flag = plundered_temple_province
							}
						}
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.421 } #enemy plunders temple
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = { owner = { NOT = { ruler_has_personality = mage_personality } } }
				province_event = { id = spirits.426 } #curiosity and the cat
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						has_ruler_flag = lightning_struck_ruler
					}
				}
				owner = { country_event = { id = spirits.428 } } # enilgtened ruler plays the flute
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.429 }	#damaged by wildlife not adventurers
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = {
					has_province_modifier = temple_complex
				}
				province_event = { id = spirits.430 }	#wisdom of merchants
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #Philosophers Demand Restoration
	id = spirits.401
	title = spirits.401.t
	desc = spirits.401.d
	picture = HIGH_TEMPLE_CITY_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		ROOT = {
			setup_temple_restoration_speed = yes
			hidden_effect = { calculate_temple_restoration = yes }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Very well
		name = spirits.401.a
		begin_temple_restoration = { owner_restorer = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				religion = high_philosophy
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			custom_tooltip = temple_restoration_cost_tt
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Suck one
		name = spirits.401.b
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { religion = high_philosophy } }
			add_province_modifier = { 
				name = spirits_denied_restoration_hp
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_province_modifier = { 
				name = spirits_denied_restoration
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #Temple Falls into Disrepair
	id = spirits.403
	title = spirits.403.t
	desc = spirits.403.d
	picture = HIGH_TEMPLE_IN_DISTANCE_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		remove_province_modifier = temple_complex
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = damaged_temple_complex
			duration = -1
		}
		downgrade_temple_wards = yes
		setup_temple_restoration_speed = yes
		ROOT = {
			setup_temple_restoration_speed = yes
			hidden_effect = { calculate_temple_restoration = yes }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Fund immediate restoration efforts
		name = spirits.403.a
		hidden_effect = { calculate_temple_restoration = yes }
		begin_temple_restoration = { owner_restorer = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				religion = high_philosophy
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			custom_tooltip = temple_restoration_cost_tt
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Damn
		name = spirits.403.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #Earthquake Strikes Temple
	id = spirits.404
	title = spirits.404.t
	desc = spirits.404.d
	picture = HIGH_TEMPLE_CITY_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = temple_complex
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
			}
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = derelict_temple_complex
				duration = -1
			}
			downgrade_temple_wards = yes
			ROOT = {
				setup_temple_restoration_speed = yes
				hidden_effect = { calculate_temple_restoration = yes }
			}
			add_devastation = 40
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Fund immediate restoration efforts
		name = spirits.404.a
		begin_temple_restoration = { owner_restorer = yes }
		tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = temple_complex
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
			}
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = derelict_temple_complex
				duration = -1
			}
			downgrade_temple_wards = yes
			setup_temple_restoration_speed = yes
			add_devastation = 40
			tooltip = {
				custom_tooltip = temple_restoration_cost_tt
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				religion = high_philosophy
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Send relief
		name = spirits.404.b
		owner = {
			add_treasury = -50
			add_adm_power = -25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_devastation = -25
		}
		tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = temple_complex
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
			}
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = derelict_temple_complex
				duration = -1
			}
			downgrade_temple_wards = yes
			setup_temple_restoration_speed = yes
			add_devastation = 15
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				religion = high_philosophy
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Damn
		name = spirits.404.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
}

#Growing attraction
province_event = {
	id = spirits.410
	title = spirits.410.t
	desc = spirits.410.d
	picture = CITY_DEVELOPMENT_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spirits.410.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_base_tax = 2
		add_base_production = 2
		add_base_manpower = 2
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					ROOT = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owned_by = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_neighbor_province = {
				add_base_tax = -1
				add_base_production = -1

		}

### Temple Quests ####

country_event = { #Temple Quest Pulse
	id = spirits.500
	title = spirits.006.t
	desc = spirits.006.d
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_temple_quest_licenses
			has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_temple_desecrators
			has_estate_privilege = estate_khelorvalshi_temple_desecrators
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = temple_quest_cooldown
			has_country_flag = temple_quest_ongoing
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
					}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = rite_of_corruption }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = azjakuma_rite_of_corruption }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = temple_heart_discovered }
				}
				religion = lefthand_path
			}
			NOT = { religion = lefthand_path }
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = first_temple_quest
	}
	
	option = { #temple quest start
		name = spirits.006.a
		trigger = { NOT = { religion = lefthand_path } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:temple_quest_target = {
					has_province_flag = restart_temple_quest
				}
			}
			event_target:temple_quest_target = {
				set_province_flag = temple_being_quested
				clr_province_flag = restart_temple_quest
				set_variable = {
					which = DaysSinceTempleEntryVar
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail } }
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail
				}
				save_event_target_as = temple_quest_target
				set_province_flag = temple_being_quested
				set_variable = {
					which = DaysSinceTempleEntryVar
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = temple_quest_target
				set_province_flag = temple_being_quested
				set_variable = {
					which = DaysSinceTempleEntryVar
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = spirits.501 days = 69 random = 420 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33 	
		}
	}
	
	option = { #temple quest start - lefthand edition
		name = spirits.006.a
		trigger = { religion = lefthand_path }
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:temple_quest_target = {
					has_province_flag = restart_temple_quest
				}
			}
			event_target:temple_quest_target = {
				set_province_flag = temple_being_quested
				clr_province_flag = restart_temple_quest
				set_variable = {
					which = DaysSinceTempleEntryVar
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail } }
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail
				}
				save_event_target_as = temple_quest_target
				set_province_flag = temple_being_quested
				set_variable = {
					which = DaysSinceTempleEntryVar
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
					}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = temple_heart_discovered }
				}
				save_event_target_as = temple_quest_target
				set_province_flag = temple_being_quested
				set_variable = {
					which = DaysSinceTempleEntryVar
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = spirits.520 days = 69 random = 420 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33

		}
	}
	
	option = { #not this time bucko
		name = spirits.006.a
		trigger = { NOT = { religion = lefthand_path } } #Don't want LHP nations to have to sit around and wait too long to be able to get to corrupting temples
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 67 
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = first_temple_quest
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Quest Preparations
	id = spirits.501
	title = spirits.501.t
	picture = EXPLORERS_eventPicture
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:temple_quest_target = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail } }
		}
		desc = spirits.501.da
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:temple_quest_target = { has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail }
		}
		desc = spirits.501.db
	}
	goto = temple_quest_target
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		always = yes
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = temple_quest_start_count
			set_country_flag = temple_quest_ongoing
			set_variable = { which = RelicsLoot value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = CoresLoot value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = RelicsLootCalculation value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = CoresLootCalculation value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = TempleQuestPartySize value = 4 }
			set_variable = { which = WoundedPartyMembers value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = RestsRemaining value = 2 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Fighter - large bonus to combat
		name = spirits.501.a
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_fighter_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { 
			temple_quest_roll_next_encounter = yes
			set_country_flag = party_leader_is_fighter
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Rogue - large bonus vs traps
		name = spirits.501.b
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_rogue_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { 
			temple_quest_roll_next_encounter = yes
			set_country_flag = party_leader_is_rogue
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Barbarian - moderate bonus to combat + small bonus vs traps
		name = spirits.501.c
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_barbarian_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { 
			temple_quest_roll_next_encounter = yes
			set_country_flag = party_leader_is_barbarian
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Monk - small bonus to combat + moderate bonus vs traps
		name = spirits.501.e
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_monk_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { 
			temple_quest_roll_next_encounter = yes
			set_country_flag = party_leader_is_monk
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Bard - small bonus to combat and traps + extra rest
		name = spirits.501.f
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_bard_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { 
			temple_quest_roll_next_encounter = yes
			set_country_flag = party_leader_is_bard
			change_variable = { which = RestsRemaining value = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Artificer - moderate bonus to combat + higher chance of salvaging Damestear Cores
		name = spirits.501.g
		trigger = { has_estate = estate_artificers }
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_artificer_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { 
			temple_quest_roll_next_encounter = yes
			set_country_flag = party_leader_is_artificer
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Update event - defeated golems version
	id = spirits.504
	title = spirits.504.t
	picture = CONQUISTADORS_eventPicture
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { religion = lefthand_path }
		}
		desc = spirits.504.da
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			religion = lefthand_path
		}
		desc = spirits.504.db
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		always = yes
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = temple_quest_lost_party_member
			clr_country_flag = temple_quest_party_member_wounded
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = salvaged_one_core_flag
		clr_country_flag = salvaged_two_cores_flag
		clr_country_flag = salvaged_three_cores_flag
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_2
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_3
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_4
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_5
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_6
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_7
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_8
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_9
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_10
	}
	
	option = { #Deeper
		name = spirits.504.a
		trigger = { NOT = { religion = lefthand_path } }
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_deeper_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { temple_quest_roll_next_encounter = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 4 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Continue - Lefthand
		name = spirits.504.ab
		trigger = { religion = lefthand_path }
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_deeper_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { temple_quest_roll_next_encounter = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 4 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Rest
		name = spirits.504.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = WoundedPartyMembers value = 1 }
			check_variable = { which = RestsRemaining value = 1 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_rest_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { 
			subtract_variable = { which = RestsRemaining value = 1 }
			temple_quest_rest = yes
			temple_quest_roll_next_encounter = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				check_variable = { which = WoundedPartyMembers value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				check_variable = { which = WoundedPartyMembers value = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Cash out - not for Lefthand because they dgaf about loot, just looking for the Heart - that's why they find it easier
		name = spirits.504.c
		trigger = { NOT = { religion = lefthand_path } }
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_voluntary_end_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			end_temple_quest = yes
			temple_quest_cash_out = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = RestsRemaining value = 1 } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = spirits.502.d
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture

		NOT = { religion = lefthand_path }
	}
	
	hidden = yes

		set_variable = { which = CoresLootCalculation which = CoresLoot }

	}

country_event = { #Hidden event to determine outcome of combat encounter
	id = spirits.510
	title = spirits.502.t
	desc = spirits.502.d
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		always = yes
	}
	
	hidden = yes
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = spirits.519 days = 3 } #Description roll
	}
	
	option = { #Win
		name = spirits.500.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 0 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 1 } }
		}
		country_event = { id = spirits.506 days = 1 } #Relics Loot Table
		country_event = { id = spirits.507 days = 2 } #Cores Salvage Table
		country_event = { id = spirits.504 days = 10 random = 3 } #Update event - defeated golems version
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 14
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_monk
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_bard
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_barbarian
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_artificer
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				has_country_flag = party_leader_is_fighter
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = party_leader_is_evoker
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Party member is wounded
		name = spirits.500.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 0 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 1 } }
		}
		subtract_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 1 }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = spirits.503 days = 180 random = 30 } #Party Wiped
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = { which = WoundedPartyMembers value = 1 }
			set_country_flag = temple_quest_party_member_wounded
			country_event = { id = spirits.506 days = 1 } #Relics Loot Table
			country_event = { id = spirits.507 days = 2 } #Cores Salvage Table
			country_event = { id = spirits.504 days = 10 random = 3 } #Update event - defeated golems version
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 4 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 3 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Lose a party member
		name = spirits.500.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 0 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = RaiseDeadRemaining value = 1 } }
			subtract_variable = { which = RaiseDeadRemaining value = 1 }
			set_country_flag = necromancer_raised_dead
		}
		else = {
			subtract_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = temple_quest_lost_party_member
		if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = spirits.503 days = 180 random = 30 } #Party Wiped
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = spirits.506 days = 1 } #Relics Loot Table
			country_event = { id = spirits.507 days = 2 } #Cores Salvage Table
			country_event = { id = spirits.504 days = 10 random = 3 } #Update event - defeated golems version
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 4 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 3 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Win
		name = spirits.500.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 1 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 2 } }
		}
		country_event = { id = spirits.506 days = 1 } #Relics Loot Table
		country_event = { id = spirits.504 days = 10 random = 3 } #Update event - defeated golems version
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 12
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_monk
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_bard
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_barbarian
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_artificer
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				has_country_flag = party_leader_is_fighter
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = party_leader_is_evoker
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Party member is wounded
		name = spirits.500.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 1 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 2 } }
		}
		subtract_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 1 }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = spirits.503 days = 180 random = 30 } #Party Wiped
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = { which = WoundedPartyMembers value = 1 }
			set_country_flag = temple_quest_party_member_wounded
			country_event = { id = spirits.506 days = 1 } #Relics Loot Table
			country_event = { id = spirits.507 days = 2 } #Cores Salvage Table
			country_event = { id = spirits.504 days = 10 random = 3 } #Update event - defeated golems version
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 6
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 4 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 3 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Lose a party member
		name = spirits.500.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 1 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 2 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = RaiseDeadRemaining value = 1 } }
			subtract_variable = { which = RaiseDeadRemaining value = 1 }
			set_country_flag = necromancer_raised_dead
		}
		else = {
			subtract_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = temple_quest_lost_party_member
		if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = spirits.503 days = 180 random = 30 } #Party Wiped
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = spirits.506 days = 1 } #Relics Loot Table
			country_event = { id = spirits.507 days = 2 } #Cores Salvage Table
			country_event = { id = spirits.504 days = 10 random = 3 } #Update event - defeated golems version
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 4 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 3 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Win
		name = spirits.500.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 2 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 3 } }
		}
		country_event = { id = spirits.506 days = 1 } #Relics Loot Table
		country_event = { id = spirits.507 days = 2 } #Cores Salvage Table
		country_event = { id = spirits.504 days = 10 random = 3 } #Update event - defeated golems version
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_monk
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_bard
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_barbarian
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_artificer
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				has_country_flag = party_leader_is_fighter
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = party_leader_is_evoker
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Party member is wounded
		name = spirits.500.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 2 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 3 } }
		}
		subtract_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 1 }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = spirits.503 days = 180 random = 30 } #Party Wiped
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = { which = WoundedPartyMembers value = 1 }
			set_country_flag = temple_quest_party_member_wounded
			country_event = { id = spirits.506 days = 1 } #Relics Loot Table
			country_event = { id = spirits.507 days = 2 } #Cores Salvage Table
			country_event = { id = spirits.504 days = 10 random = 3 } #Update event - defeated golems version
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 7
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 4 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 3 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Lose a party member

country_event = {	#Roll to determine next encounter - add new encounters here 
	id = spirits.516
	title = spirits.502.t
	desc = spirits.502.d
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		always = yes
	}
	
	option = { 
		country_event = { id = spirits.510 days = 1 } #Combat with golems
		set_country_flag = golem_encounter_flag
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		country_event = { id = spirits.511 days = 1 } #Trap
		set_country_flag = trap_encounter_flag
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { religion = lefthand_path }
			check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 3 }
			event_target:temple_quest_target = {
				NOT = {
					has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex
					has_province_modifier = temple_heart_discovered
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = spirits.517 days = 1 } #Heart Chamber
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				event_target:temple_quest_target = { has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 4 } 
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 5 } 
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 6 } 
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			religion = lefthand_path
			check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 4 }
		}
		country_event = { id = spirits.517 days = 1 } #Heart Chamber
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				event_target:temple_quest_target = { has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail }
				check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 3 } 
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 4 } 
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 5 } 
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				check_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 6 } 
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Roll to determine outcome of Heart Chamber encounter
	id = spirits.517
	title = spirits.502.t
	desc = spirits.502.d
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		always = yes
	}
	
	hidden = yes
	
	option = { #Clear the room
		country_event = { id = spirits.506 days = 1 } #Relics Loot Table
		country_event = { id = spirits.507 days = 2 } #Cores Salvage Table
		if = {
			limit = { religion = lefthand_path }
			country_event = { id = spirits.601 days = 10 random = 3 }
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = spirits.518 days = 10 random = 3 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_monk
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_bard
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_barbarian
					has_country_flag = party_leader_is_artificer
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				has_country_flag = party_leader_is_fighter
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = party_leader_is_evoker
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Wipe
		country_event = { id = spirits.503 days = 180 random = 30 } #Party Wiped | please stop breaking
		if = { limit = { NOT = { event_target:temple_quest_target = { has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail } } }
			event_target:temple_quest_target = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = temple_heart_trail
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 4 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 3 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.8
				NOT = { check_variable = { which =  TempleQuestPartySize value = 2 } }
			}
			modifier = { #The last party probably killed a few of the golems in the chamber
				factor = 0.5
				event_target:temple_quest_target = { has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Update event - Discovered Heart Chamber
	id = spirits.518
	title = spirits.518.t
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = temple_heart_knowledge_unlocked
		}
		desc = spirits.518.da
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = temple_heart_knowledge_unlocked }
		}
		desc = spirits.518.db
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		always = yes
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = temple_quest_lost_party_member
			clr_country_flag = temple_quest_party_member_wounded
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_2
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_3
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_4
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_5
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_6
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_7
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_8
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_9
		clr_country_flag = looted_relics_10
		clr_country_flag = salvaged_one_core_flag
		clr_country_flag = salvaged_two_cores_flag
		clr_country_flag = salvaged_three_cores_flag
	}
	
	option = { #Return home with this knowledge
		name = spirits.518.a
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_discovered_heart_chamber_tooltip
		temple_quest_cash_out = yes
		event_target:temple_quest_target = { province_event = { id = spirits.012 } } #Heart Discovery
		hidden_effect = {
			discover_heart_chamber = yes
			end_temple_quest = yes
			set_country_flag = temple_heart_knowledge_unlocked
		}
	}
}

		}

country_event = { #Quest Preparations - Lefthand Version
	id = spirits.520
	title = spirits.520.t
	picture = EXPLORERS_eventPicture
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:temple_quest_target = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail } }
		}
		desc = spirits.520.da
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:temple_quest_target = { has_province_modifier = temple_heart_trail }
		}
		desc = spirits.520.db
	}
	goto = temple_quest_target
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		always = yes
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = temple_quest_start_count
			set_country_flag = temple_quest_ongoing
			set_variable = { which = TempleQuestFloor value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = TempleQuestPartySize value = 4 }
			set_variable = { which = WoundedPartyMembers value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = RestsRemaining value = 2 }
			set_variable = { which = RaiseDeadRemaining value = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Evoker - formidable bonus to combat
		name = spirits.520.a
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_evoker_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { 
			temple_quest_roll_next_encounter = yes
			set_country_flag = party_leader_is_evoker
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Diviner - formidable bonus vs traps
		name = spirits.520.b
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_diviner_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { 
			temple_quest_roll_next_encounter = yes
			set_country_flag = party_leader_is_diviner
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Necromancer - 3 uses of Raise Dead
		name = spirits.520.c
		custom_tooltip = temple_quest_necromancer_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { 
			temple_quest_roll_next_encounter = yes
			set_country_flag = party_leader_is_necromancer
			change_variable = { which = RaiseDeadRemaining value = 3 }
		}
	}
}

#Secret of the Temples - catchall event to give LHP tags without MTs the ability to unlock Temple Corruption
country_event = {
	id = spirits.600
	title = spirits.600.t
	picture = BIG_BOOK_eventPicture
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				any_ally = {
					tag = Y01
				}
				is_subject_of = Y01
			}
		}
		desc = spirits.600.da
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owns_core_province = 5430
				owns_core_province = 4829
				owns_core_province = 4831
				owns_core_province = 4828
				owns_core_province = 4848
			}
		}
		desc = spirits.600.db
	}
	
	trigger = {
		religion = lefthand_path
		NOT = { #Add tags here who get this flag via MT
			has_country_flag = lefthand_temple_secrets
			tag = Y01 #Azjakuma - Oni already know this shit
		}
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = temple_complex
				has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
				has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
			}
		}
		OR = {
			OR = {
				owns_core_province = 5430
				owns_core_province = 4829
				owns_core_province = 4831
				owns_core_province = 4828
				owns_core_province = 4848
			}
			OR = {
				any_ally = {
					tag = Y01
				}
				is_subject_of = Y01
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 180
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 5
				region = demon_hills_region
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				region = demon_hills_region
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			Y01 = {
				has_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			Y01 = {
				has_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 150
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = lefthand_temple_secrets }
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = spirits.600.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				any_ally = { tag = Y01 }
				is_subject_of = Y01
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = lefthand_temple_secrets_unlock_tooltip
		add_mil_power = -25
		add_dip_power = -25
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = spirits.600.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_ally = { tag = Y01 }
				is_subject_of = Y01
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = lefthand_temple_secrets_unlock_tooltip
		add_adm_power = -50
	}
}

country_event = { #Temple Corruption menu
	id = spirits.602
	title = spirits.602.t
	desc = spirits.602.d
	picture = RAMADAN_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { define_temple_to_corrupt = yes }
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = corrupt_@ROOT }
				clr_province_flag = corrupt_@ROOT
				clr_province_flag = option_corrupt_1_@ROOT
				clr_province_flag = option_corrupt_2_@ROOT
				clr_province_flag = option_corrupt_3_@ROOT
				clr_province_flag = option_corrupt_4_@ROOT
				clr_province_flag = option_corrupt_5_@ROOT
				clr_province_flag = option_corrupt_6_@ROOT

		}

        name = spirits.602.a

province_event = {	#Temple Corrupted
	id = spirits.603
	title = spirits.603.t
	desc = spirits.603.d
	picture = RAMADAN_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_province_modifier = rite_of_corruption
			has_province_modifier = azjakuma_rite_of_corruption
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = CorruptedHeartMana value = 0 } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = temple_complex }
			hidden_effect = {
				corrupt_temple_wards = yes
				set_province_flag = was_temple_complex
			}
			remove_province_modifier = temple_complex
			add_province_triggered_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex }
			hidden_effect = {
				corrupt_temple_wards = yes
				set_province_flag = was_damaged_temple_complex
			}
			remove_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
			add_province_triggered_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex }
			hidden_effect = {
				corrupt_temple_wards = yes
				set_province_flag = was_derelict_temple_complex
			}
			remove_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
			add_province_triggered_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
		}
		owner = {
			hidden_effect = {
				every_known_country = {
					limit = {
						capital_scope = {
							continent = asia
							NOT = { superregion = forbidden_lands_superregion }
						}
						NOT = { alliance_with = PREV }
						NOT = { religion = lefthand_path }
						NOT = { is_subject_of = PREV }
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = PREV
						modifier = spirits_corrupted_temple
					}
					remove_opinion = { #so you don't double up on negative opinion modifiers
						who = PREV
						modifier = spirits_corrupted_temple_ally
					}
				}
				every_known_country = {
					limit = {
						alliance_with = PREV
						capital_scope = {
							continent = asia
							NOT = { superregion = forbidden_lands_superregion }
						}
						NOT = { religion = lefthand_path }
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = PREV
						modifier = spirits_corrupted_temple_ally
					}
					remove_opinion = { #so you don't double up on negative opinion modifiers
						who = PREV
						modifier = spirits_corrupted_temple
					}
				}
			}
		}
		remove_province_modifier = rite_of_corruption
		remove_province_modifier = azjakuma_rite_of_corruption
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.603.a
		goto = ROOT
		custom_tooltip = temple_corrupted_tt
		custom_tooltip = spirits_corrupted_temple_opinion_tooltip
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_known_country = { 
						alliance_with = PREV
						capital_scope = {
							continent = asia
							NOT = { superregion = forbidden_lands_superregion }
						}
						NOT = { religion = lefthand_path }
					}
				}  
				custom_tooltip = spirits_corrupted_temple_opinion_ally_tooltip
			}
		}
	}
}

		set_province_flag = spirit_bound
	}
	option = { #Minor Spirit Bound
		name = spirits.604.a
		province_event = { id = spirits.605 }
		set_province_flag = minor_spirit_bound
	}
}

country_event = {	#Draining the Heart
	id = spirits.606
	title = spirits.606.t
	desc = spirits.606.d
	picture = RAMADAN_eventPicture
	goto = corrupted_temple_drain_target
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = in_heart_drain_menu }
			has_country_flag = in_deeper_heart_drain_menu
		}
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = corrupted_heart_drain_cooldown }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = in_heart_drain_menu
		clr_country_flag = in_deeper_heart_drain_menu
	}
	
	option = {	#Cast a Sinister Ritual
		name = spirits.606.a
		country_event = { id = spirits.608 }	#Sinister Ritual menu
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = in_deeper_heart_drain_menu }
	}
	
	option = {	#UNLIMITED POWER!
		name = spirits.606.b
		trigger = { has_regency = no has_consort_regency = no }
		country_event = { id = spirits.609 }	#Unlimited Power menu
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = in_deeper_heart_drain_menu }	
	}
	
	option = {	#Empower a War Wizard
		name = spirits.606.c
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = spirits_war_wizard_cooldown } }
		create_war_wizard_effect = yes
		lhp_heart_drain_choose_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = spirits_war_wizard_cooldown_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = spirits_war_wizard_cooldown
				duration = 18250 #50 years
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {	#Empower Prominent Court Sorcerer
		name = spirits.606.e
		define_advisor = {
			type = court_mage
			skill = 4
			cost_multiplier = 0.25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = Y01 }
			}
			add_estate_loyalty_modifier = {

country_event = {	#Check to see if any corrupted hearts are ready to drain
	id = spirits.607
	title = spirits.606.t
	desc = spirits.606.d
	picture = GOLDEN_CITY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		religion = lefthand_path
		any_owned_province = {
			has_active_triggered_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
			check_variable = { which = CorruptedHeartMana value = 10 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = spirits.607.a
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_active_triggered_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
				check_variable = { which = CorruptedHeartMana value = 10 }
			}
			save_event_target_as = corrupted_temple_drain_target
		}
		country_event = { id = spirits.606 days = 1 }
	}
}
	
country_event = {	#A Sinister Ritual
	id = spirits.608
	title = spirits.608.t
	desc = spirits.608.d
	picture = END_OF_TIME_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	option = {	#Eldritch Foresight
		name = spirits.608.a
		increase_witch_king_points_large = yes
		add_ruler_modifier = {
			name = lefthand_eldritch_foresight
			duration = 90
		}
		lhp_heart_drain_choose_option = yes
	}
	
	option = {	#Unnatural Plant Growth
		name = spirits.608.b
		increase_witch_king_points_large = yes
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { province_with_farm_goods = yes }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = lefthand_unnatural_plant_growth
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
		lhp_heart_drain_choose_option = yes
	}
	
	option = {	#Epic Raise Dead
		name = spirits.608.c
		increase_witch_king_points_large = yes
		add_yearly_manpower = 1
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = lefthand_epic_raise_dead
			duration = 1825
		}
		lhp_heart_drain_choose_option = yes
	}
	
	option = {	#Summon a Damestear Meteor
		name = spirits.608.e
		increase_witch_king_points_large = yes
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					province_group = temple_province_group
					trade_goods = damestear
				}
			}
			change_trade_goods = damestear
			add_base_tax = -3
			add_base_production = -3
			add_base_manpower = -3
			add_devastation = 20
		}
		lhp_heart_drain_choose_option = yes
	}
	
	#Go Back
	option = {
        name = spirits.602.h
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		country_event = { id = spirits.606 }
	}
}

country_event = {	#Unlimited Power
	id = spirits.609
	title = spirits.609.t
	desc = spirits.609.d
	picture = GREAT_MAN_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	immediate = { #there is probably already a flag for this
		if = {
			limit = { ruler_has_personality = mage_personality }
			set_ruler_flag = spirits_mage_ruler
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_long_lived_ruler = yes }
			set_ruler_flag = spirits_immortal_ruler
		}
	}

	after = {
		clr_ruler_flag = spirits_mage_ruler
		clr_ruler_flag = spirits_immortal_ruler
	}
	
	option = {	#an Expanded Mind
		name = spirits.609.a
		trigger = { NOT = { adm = 6 } }
		change_adm = 1
		lhp_heart_drain_choose_option = yes
	}
	
	option = {	#an Enthralling Soul
		name = spirits.609.b
		trigger = { NOT = { dip = 6 } }
		change_dip = 1
		lhp_heart_drain_choose_option = yes
	}
	
	option = {	#a Mighty Will
		name = spirits.609.c
		trigger = { NOT = { mil = 6 } }
		change_mil = 1
		lhp_heart_drain_choose_option = yes
	}
	
	option = {	#an Infusion of Chi
		name = spirits.609.e
		trigger = { ruler_has_mage_personality = yes }
		add_adm_power = 75
		add_dip_power = 75
		add_mil_power = 75
		lhp_heart_drain_choose_option = yes
	}
	
	option = {	#an Infusion of Power
		name = spirits.609.f
		trigger = { NOT = { ruler_has_mage_personality = yes } }
		if = {
			limit = { ruler_has_max_personalities = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				clear_ruler_personalities = yes
				# Restore lost personalities
				if = {
					limit = { has_ruler_flag = spirits_immortal_ruler }
					set_ruler_flag = immortal_ruler
				}
			}
		}
		force_add_ruler_personality = { personality = mage_personality }
		lhp_heart_drain_choose_option = yes
	}
	
	option = {	#Life extension
	#Allows lhp mage rulers to extend their life, has diminishing returns
	#extended to 110, 140, 160, 175, 185, 190, 195, can not live past ~200
	#not that worth it past 175
	#kill event is hooked into the racial death event, in order to avoid using VAT or export_to_variable
	#the ages for death are hardcoded, so all of them need to be changed to adjust life extension duration
	name = spirits.609.g
	trigger = { 
		ruler_has_mage_personality = yes
		has_country_flag = lefthand_life_extension_unlocked
		NOT = { has_ruler_flag = is_a_lich }
		NOT = { has_ruler_flag = is_a_vampire } #Its pointless if you go lich or vampire
		NOT = { is_variable_equal = { which = lefthand_life_extension_max_age_var value = 190 } }
	}
	
	set_ruler_flag = long_lived_ruler

	custom_tooltip = spirits_life_extension_option_tooltip

	hidden_effect = { #I know this is bad, but it shouldn't hurt performance and I don't know what the hell I'm doing
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_ruler_flag = lefthand_life_extension }
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = lefthand_life_extension_max_age_var
				value = 110 #extends life to 120 years
			}
			set_ruler_flag = lefthand_life_extension
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_ruler_flag = lefthand_life_extension
				is_variable_equal = { #make sure it is selecting the correct life extension
					which = lefthand_life_extension_max_age_var
					value = 110
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = lefthand_life_extension_max_age_var
				value = 30 #adds another 30 years, continues for the rest of these
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_ruler_flag = lefthand_life_extension
				is_variable_equal = { #make sure it is selecting the correct life extension
					which = lefthand_life_extension_max_age_var
					value = 140
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = lefthand_life_extension_max_age_var
				value = 20
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_ruler_flag = lefthand_life_extension
				is_variable_equal = { #make sure it is selecting the correct life extension
					which = lefthand_life_extension_max_age_var
					value = 160
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = lefthand_life_extension_max_age_var
				value = 15
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_ruler_flag = lefthand_life_extension
				is_variable_equal = { #make sure it is selecting the correct life extension
					which = lefthand_life_extension_max_age_var
					value = 175
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = lefthand_life_extension_max_age_var
				value = 10 #increase life extension
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_ruler_flag = lefthand_life_extension
				is_variable_equal = {
					which = lefthand_life_extension_max_age_var
					value = 185
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = lefthand_life_extension_max_age_var
				value = 5
			}
		}
	}
	
	lhp_heart_drain_choose_option = yes
}

	#Go Back
	option = {
        name = spirits.602.h
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		country_event = { id = spirits.606 }
	}
}

#catchall event to give any non-Azjakuma country the ability to extend life
country_event = {
	id = spirits.622
	title = spirits.622.t
	desc = spirits.622.d
	picture = BIG_BOOK_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		religion = lefthand_path
		NOT = { #Add tags here who get this flag via MT
			has_country_flag = lefthand_life_extension_unlocked
			tag = Y01 #Azjakuma - Oni already know this shit
		}
		any_owned_province = {
			has_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
		}
		owns_core_province = 4848
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 180
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 5
				region = demon_hills_region
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				region = demon_hills_region
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			Y01 = {
				has_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			Y01 = {
				has_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 150
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = lefthand_life_extension_unlocked }
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = spirits.622.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				any_ally = { tag = Y01 }
				is_subject_of = Y01
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = lefthand_temple_secrets_unlock_tooltip
		add_mil_power = -25
		add_dip_power = -25
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = spirits.622.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_ally = { tag = Y01 }
				is_subject_of = Y01
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = lefthand_temple_secrets_unlock_tooltip
		add_adm_power = -50
	}

country_event = { #maybe add soemthing so you can always summon at the last temple you summoned at
	id = spirits.625
	title = spirits.625.t
	picture = RAMADAN_eventPicture
	desc = spirits.625.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { define_temple_to_summon = yes }
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = summon_@ROOT }
				clr_province_flag = summon_@ROOT
				clr_province_flag = option_summon_1_@ROOT
				clr_province_flag = option_summon_2_@ROOT
				clr_province_flag = option_summon_3_@ROOT
				clr_province_flag = option_summon_4_@ROOT
				clr_province_flag = option_summon_5_@ROOT
				clr_province_flag = option_summon_6_@ROOT
				remove_province_modifier = lhp_summon_same_temple
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
        name = spirits.625.a
        ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		trigger = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = option_summon_1_@ROOT } }
		goto = summon1
		event_target:summon1 = {
			hidden_effect = { save_event_target_as = summonTarget }
			province_event = { id = spirits.626 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
        name = spirits.625.b
        ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		trigger = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = option_summon_2_@ROOT } }
		goto = summon2
		event_target:summon2 = {
			hidden_effect = { save_event_target_as = summonTarget }
			province_event = { id = spirits.626 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
        name = spirits.625.c
        ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		trigger = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = option_summon_3_@ROOT } }
		goto = summon3
		event_target:summon3 = {
			hidden_effect = { save_event_target_as = summonTarget }
			province_event = { id = spirits.626 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
        name = spirits.625.e
        ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		trigger = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = option_summon_4_@ROOT } }
		goto = summon4
		event_target:summon4 = {
			hidden_effect = { save_event_target_as = summonTarget }
			province_event = { id = spirits.626 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
        name = spirits.625.f
        ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		trigger = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = option_summon_5_@ROOT } }
		goto = summon5
		event_target:summon5 = {
			hidden_effect = { save_event_target_as = summonTarget }
			province_event = { id = spirits.626 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
        name = spirits.625.g
        ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		trigger = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = option_summon_6_@ROOT } }
		goto = summon6

		}

	}

province_event = { #spirit summoning
	id = spirits.626 #costs and shit need to be added
	title = spirits.626.t
	picture = RAMADAN_eventPicture
	desc = spirits.626.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		#set which shirgrii does it, not relevant for other lhp countries
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { tag = Y01 } }
			random_list = {
				20 = { 
					trigger = { owner = { has_estate = estate_shinukhorchi estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_shinukhorchi loyalty = 60 } } } 
					owner = { set_country_flag = shinukhorchi_summon }
				}
				20 = { 
					trigger = { owner = { has_estate = estate_chumijemoya estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_chumijemoya loyalty = 60 } } } 
					owner = { set_country_flag = chumijemoya_summon }
				}
				20 = { 
					trigger = { owner = { has_estate = estate_ajgriijarul estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_ajgriijarul loyalty = 60 } } } 
					owner = { set_country_flag = ajgriijarul_summon }
				}
				20 = { 
					trigger = { owner = { has_estate = estate_kabiurgarko estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_kabiurgarko loyalty = 60 } } } 
					owner = { set_country_flag = kabiurgarko_summon }
				}
				20 = { 
					trigger = { owner = { has_estate = estate_khelorvalshi estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_khelorvalshi loyalty = 60 } } } 
					owner = { set_country_flag = khelorvalshi_summon }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #close
		name = spirits.626.a
		owner = { clr_country_flag = temple_summoning_menu_open }
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.626.b
		custom_tooltip = spirits_summon_minor_tooltip
		owner = { add_church_power = -5 }
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:summonTarget = {
				set_province_flag = minor_spirit_bound
				province_event = {
					id = spirits.627
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = lhp_summon_cooldown
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #chance of failing, small penalty
		name = spirits.626.c

		custom_tooltip = spirits_summon_normal_tooltip
		owner = { add_church_power = -10 }
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = { set_country_flag = spirits_summon_medium_random }
			province_event = { id = spirits.631 }
		}

		owner = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = lhp_summon_cooldown
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #larger chance of failing, large penalty
		name = spirits.626.e

		custom_tooltip = spirits_summon_powerful_tooltip
		owner = { add_church_power = -15 }
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = { set_country_flag = spirits_summon_powerful_random }
			province_event = { id = spirits.631 }
		}

		owner = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = lhp_summon_cooldown
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}
