province_event = { #medium summon failure
	id = spirits.628 #can be changed to differet descs later
	title = spirits.628.t
	picture = RAMADAN_eventPicture
	desc = spirits.628.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		always = yes
	}

	after = {
		owner = {
			clr_country_flag = spirits_summon_medium_random
			clr_country_flag = spirits_summon_powerful_random
			clr_country_flag = temple_summoning_menu_open
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = lhp_summon_same_temple
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {	#Thank you very cool
		name = spirits.628.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_1
						has_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_2
					}
				}
			}
			owner = { set_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_1
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_2
					}
				}
			}
			owner = { set_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_2 }
			owner = { clr_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_2
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_3
					}
				}
			}
			owner = { set_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_3 }
			owner = { clr_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_3
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_4
					}
				}
			}
			owner = { set_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_4 }
			owner = { clr_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_3 }
		}
		owner = { clr_country_flag = temple_summoning_menu_open }
		
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate = estate_mages }
				add_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
					estate = estate_mages
					loyalty = -5
					duration = 3650
					desc = medium_summon_failed_desc
				}
				add_estate_influence_modifier = {
					estate = estate_mages
					influence = -33
					duration = 3650
					desc = medium_summon_failed_desc
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = shinukhorchi_summon }
				add_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
					estate = estate_shinukhorchi
					loyalty = -5
					duration = 3650
					desc = medium_summon_failed_desc
				}
				add_estate_influence_modifier = {
					estate = estate_shinukhorchi
					influence = -33
					duration = 3650
					desc = medium_summon_failed_desc
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = chumijemoya_summon }
				add_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
					estate = estate_chumijemoya
					loyalty = -5
					duration = 3650
					desc = medium_summon_failed_desc
				}
				add_estate_influence_modifier = {
					estate = estate_chumijemoya
					influence = -33
					duration = 3650
					desc = medium_summon_failed_desc
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ajgriijarul_summon }
				add_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
					estate = estate_ajgriijarul
					loyalty = -5
					duration = 3650
					desc = medium_summon_failed_desc
				}
				add_estate_influence_modifier = {
					estate = estate_ajgriijarul
					influence = -33
					duration = 3650
					desc = medium_summon_failed_desc
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = kabiurgarko_summon }
				add_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
					estate = estate_kabiurgarko
					loyalty = -5
					duration = 3650
					desc = medium_summon_failed_desc
				}
				add_estate_influence_modifier = {
					estate = estate_kabiurgarko
					influence = -33
					duration = 3650
					desc = medium_summon_failed_desc
				}
			}
			else_if = {

			}
		}
	}

		name = spirits.626.e

			}

				factor = 0.55
				owner = { has_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				owner = { has_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.85
				owner = { has_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_3 }
			}
		}
		event_target:summonTarget = {
			set_province_flag = powerful_spirit_bound
			province_event = {
				id = spirits.627
				days = 30
			}
		}
		owner = { clr_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_1 }
		owner = { clr_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_2 }
		owner = { clr_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_3 }
		owner = { clr_country_flag = lhp_pity_medium_4 }
	}

		name = spirits.631.g
		trigger = { owner = { has_country_flag = spirits_summon_powerful_random } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {

			}

# rending start, hidden event
country_event = {
	id = spirits.700
	title = spirits.700.t
	desc = spirits.700.d
	picture = BIG_BOOK_eventPicture

	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		current_age = age_of_absolutism
		owns = 4871
		NOT = { has_global_flag = rending_active }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			NOT = {
				4871 = {
					check_variable = {
						which = globalWardStrength
						value = 50
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.90
			NOT = {
				4871 = {
					check_variable = {
						which = globalWardStrength
						value = 45
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			NOT = {
				4871 = {
					check_variable = {
						which = globalWardStrength
						value = 40
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.80
			NOT = {
				4871 = {
					check_variable = {
						which = globalWardStrength
						value = 35
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.50
			NOT = {
				4871 = {
					check_variable = {
						which = globalWardStrength
						value = 30
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			is_year = 1655
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.700.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

		set_global_flag = rending_active
		every_country = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_province = {
						OR = {
							has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
							has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
							has_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = spirits.701 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { any_owned_province = { continent = asia NOT = { superregion = forbidden_lands_superregion } } }
				country_event = { id = spirits.702 days = 180 }
			}
		}
	}

# RENDING HAS STARTED, GLOBAL EVENT
country_event = {
	id = spirits.703
	title = spirits.703.t
	desc = spirits.703.d
	picture = GREAT_SPIRIT_YANHE_eventPicture

	trigger = {
        OR = {
            Y26 = { mission_completed = Y26_huszien_restored }
            had_global_flag = {
                flag = rending_active
                days = 360
            }
        }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = rending_started_country }
		OR = {
			capital_scope = {
				continent = asia
				NOT = { superregion = forbidden_lands_superregion }
			}
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				continent = asia
				NOT = { superregion = forbidden_lands_superregion }
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = rending_started_country
			temple_province_group = {
				limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
				spirit_swarms = 2
				if = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = temple_complex }
					random_list = {
						35 = {
							remove_province_modifier = temple_complex
							add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = damaged_temple_complex duration = -1 }
							downgrade_temple_wards = yes
						}
						15 = {
							remove_province_modifier = temple_complex
							add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = derelict_temple_complex duration = -1 }
							downgrade_temple_wards = yes
						}
						50 = {}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex }
					add_devastation = 25
					every_neighbor_province = { add_devastation = 10 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex }
					add_devastation = 50
					every_neighbor_province = { add_devastation = 15 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex }
					add_devastation = 75
					every_neighbor_province = { add_devastation = 20 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex }
					add_devastation = 100
					spirit_swarms = 3
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					continent = asia
					NOT = { superregion = forbidden_lands_superregion }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 20
					add_devastation = 5
				}
				random = {
					chance = 2
					spirit_swarms = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						religion = bangujonsi
						religion = mystic_accord
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = rending_appease_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					religion = lefthand_path
				}
				set_country_flag = rending_corrupt_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { religion = righteous_path } # righteous path gets an event to choose
				}
				set_country_flag = rending_ward_flag
			}
			4559 = {
				set_variable = {
					which = rendingMonthsLeft
					value = 480
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = rending_startup_complete } }
				asia = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { 
							superregion = forbidden_lands_superregion
							superregion = north_haless_superregion
							has_province_flag = pristine_wards
						}
					}
					add_permanent_province_modifier = {
						name = rending_unhindered_spirits
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			hokuma_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }

			yanhe_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }

			kharunyana_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }

			phokhao_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }

			hengdu_bowu_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }

			cinulau_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }

			lupulan_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }

			dhenbasana_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }

			marutha_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }

			gehet_ketine_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }

			hukai_telebei_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }

			huszien_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }

			tughayasa_spirit_area = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rending_domain_helper duration = -1 } }
			
			
			country_event = {
				id = spirits.1002
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #high philosophy + all other religions basically
		name = spirits.703.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { has_country_flag = rending_ward_flag }

		custom_tooltip = stop_rending_ward

		custom_tooltip = spirits_bork_temple_tt
		custom_tooltip = spirits_break_temple_tt

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = rending_severe_global
			duration = -1
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy }
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_no_ma_tooltip
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { religion = mystic_accord }
					remove_province_modifier = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = spirits.705 days = 30 } }
	}
	option = { #mystic accord
		name = spirits.703.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { has_country_flag = rending_appease_flag }

		custom_tooltip = stop_rending_appease

		custom_tooltip = spirits_bork_temple_tt
		custom_tooltip = spirits_break_temple_tt

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = rending_medium_global
			duration = -1
		}
		country_event = { 
			id = rending.300
			days = 20
		}
	}
	option = { #rightous path
		name = spirits.703.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { religion = righteous_path }

		custom_tooltip = spirits_bork_temple_tt
		custom_tooltip = spirits_break_temple_tt
		country_event = { id = spirits.704 }
	}
	option = { #lefthand path
		name = spirits.703.e
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { has_country_flag = rending_corrupt_flag }

		custom_tooltip = stop_rending_scour

		custom_tooltip = spirits_bork_temple_tt
		custom_tooltip = spirits_break_temple_tt

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = rending_severe_global
			duration = -1
		}

		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = spirits.705 days = 30 } }
	}
}

						hengdu_bowu_spirit_area = { owner = { country_event = { id = spirits.712 } } }
						cinulau_spirit_area = { owner = { country_event = { id = spirits.713 } } }
						lupulan_spirit_area = { owner = { country_event = { id = spirits.714 } } }

						marutha_spirit_area = { owner = { country_event = { id = spirits.716 } } }

			}
			custom_tooltip = tughayasa_unowned_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					tughayasa_spirit_area = {
						type = all
						OR = {
							has_province_flag = pristine_wards
							area_for_scope_province = { has_state_edict = spirit_hunters_edict }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = spirit_region_not_warded
		}
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					4527 = {
						OR = {
							has_province_flag = pristine_wards
							area_for_scope_province = { has_state_edict = spirit_hunters_edict }
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = { owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 4527 }
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = tughayasa_suppressed }
		}
		remove_rending_highlight = yes
		set_country_flag = tughayasa_highlight
	}
	option = { #four lords disabled option
		name = spirits.706.27
		set_country_flag = spirit_disabled_option
		custom_tooltip = spirit_ward_region_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					huszien_spirit_area = {
						type = all
						OR = {
							has_province_flag = pristine_wards
							area_for_scope_province = { has_state_edict = spirit_hunters_edict }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = spirit_region_not_warded
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 4923 }
					NOT = { owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 4915 }
					NOT = { owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 4877 }
					NOT = { owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 4891 }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = four_lords_unowned_tt
		}
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = huszien_resurrected }
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					huszien_spirit_area = {
						type = all
						OR = {
							has_province_flag = pristine_wards
							area_for_scope_province = { has_state_edict = spirit_hunters_edict }
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = { owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 4923 }
				NOT = { owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 4915 }
				NOT = { owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 4877 }
				NOT = { owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 4891 }
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = huszien_suppressed }
			
		}
		remove_rending_highlight = yes
		set_country_flag = huszien_highlight
	}
	option = { #back
		name = spirits.706.b
		highlight = yes
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = spirit_disabled_option }
				country_event = { id = spirits.707 }
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = halessi_spirit_menu_flag
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = spirits.707
	title = spirits.707.t
	desc = spirits.707.d
	picture = EMPTY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = spirits.707.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = spirit_disabled_option }
			country_event = { id = spirits.706 }
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = scour_disabled_option }
			country_event = { id = spirits.736 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = spirits.721
	title = spirits.721.t
	desc = spirits.721.d
	picture = DARK_FOREST_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			hokuma_spirit_area = {
				remove_province_modifier = rending_unhindered_spirits
				add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = spirit_region_warded duration = -1 }
			}
			set_global_flag = hokuma_suppressed
			spirit_end_rending_if_applicable = yes

			set_global_flag = disable_hokuma
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.721.a
		custom_tooltip = suppress_1_tt
		custom_tooltip = no_more_bad_spirit_tt

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = hokuma_suppressed_modifier
			duration = -1
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

# REND END HIDDEN
country_event = {
	id = spirits.734
	title = spirits.734.t
	desc = spirits.734.d
	picture = GREAT_SPIRIT_TELEBEI_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		had_global_flag = {
			flag = rending_active
			days = 900
		}
		4559 = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = rendingMonthsLeft
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = rending_active
			every_country = {
				remove_country_modifier = hokuma_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = yanhe_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = kharunyana_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = phokhao_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = hengdu_bowu_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = cinulau_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = lupulan_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = dhenbasana_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = marutha_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = gehet_ketine_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = hukai_telebei_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = huszien_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = huli_jing_suppressed_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = hokuma_scoured_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = yanhe_scoured_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = kharunyana_scoured_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = phokhao_scoured_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = hengdu_bowu_scoured_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = cinulau_scoured_modifier
				remove_country_modifier = lupulan_scoured_modifier

#######################################
###      GREAT SPIRITS SCOURED      ###

#Hokuma Suppressed
country_event = {
	id = spirits.737
	title = spirits.737.t
	desc = spirits.737.d
	picture = GREAT_SPIRIT_HOKUMA_EVIL_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			hokuma_spirit_area = {
				set_province_flag = rending_scoured_flag
				remove_province_modifier = rending_unhindered_spirits
				add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = spirit_region_warded duration = -1 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = hokuma_scouring
			set_global_flag = hokuma_scoured
			spirit_end_rending_if_applicable = yes

			set_global_flag = disable_hokuma
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.737.a
		custom_tooltip = scour_1_tt
		custom_tooltip = no_more_bad_spirit_tt

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = hokuma_scoured_modifier
			duration = -1
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

	picture = GREAT_SPIRIT_GEHET_KETINE_EVIL_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			gehet_ketine_spirit_area = {
				set_province_flag = rending_scoured_flag
				remove_province_modifier = rending_unhindered_spirits
				add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = spirit_region_warded duration = -1 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = gehet_ketine_scouring
			set_global_flag = gehet_ketine_scoured
			spirit_end_rending_if_applicable = yes

			set_global_flag = disable_gehet_ketine
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.746.a
		custom_tooltip = scour_10_tt
		custom_tooltip = no_more_bad_spirit_tt

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gehet_ketine_scoured_modifier
			duration = -1
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

#Scouring Finished Event Manager
country_event = {
	id = spirits.751
	title = spirits.751.t
	desc = spirits.751.d
	picture = ONI_HUMANS_eventPicture

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = rending_active
		had_country_flag = {
			flag = is_scouring_domain
			days = 912
		}
	}

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_country_flag
				hokuma_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.737 } }
				yanhe_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.738 } }
				kharunyana_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.739 } }
				phokhao_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.740 } }
				hengdu_bowu_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.741 } }
				cinulau_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.742 } }
				lupulan_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.743 } }
				dhenbasana_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.744 } }
				marutha_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.745 } }
				gehet_ketine_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.746 } }
				hukai_telebei_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.747 } }
				huszien_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.748 } }
				tughayasa_scouring = { country_event = { id = spirits.749 } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.751.a
		custom_tooltip = spirit_scour_region_tt

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

#Bianfang goes MA
country_event = {
	id = spirits.1000
	title = spirits.1000.t
	desc = spirits.1000.d
	picture = GREAT_SPIRIT_YANHE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spirits.1000.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_heir = yes
			}
			kill_heir = {}
		}
		capital_scope = {
			spirit_swarms = 3
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			spirit_swarms = 2
		}
		add_stability = -1
	}
	option = {
		name = spirits.1000.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
		change_religion = mystic_accord
		add_stability = -4
		if = {
			limit = {
				ai = no
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = yanhe_chosen
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = yanhe_chosen_ai
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = rending_ward_flag
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = rending_medium_global
				duration = -1
			}
			set_country_flag = rending_appease_flag
			set_country_flag = appeasement_in_progress
			set_country_flag = yanhe_appeasement
			set_country_flag = yanhe_primary
			remove_country_modifier = rending_severe_global
		}
	}
}

#Ward North Haless - Jiantsiang
province_event = {
	id = spirits.1001
	title = spirits.1001.t
	desc = spirits.1001.d
	picture = GREAT_SPIRIT_YANHE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = spirits.1001.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = temple_of_undying_flame
					tier = 2
				}
			}
			shuvuushudi_region = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = pristine_wards } }
				set_province_flag = damaged_wards
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = temple_of_undying_flame
					tier = 3
				}
			}
			shuvuushudi_region = {
				clr_province_flag = damaged_wards
				set_province_flag = pristine_wards
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Kharunyana destroys the Godswall
	id = spirits.1002
	title = spirits.1002.t
	desc = spirits.1002.desc
	picture = GREAT_SPIRIT_KHARUNYANA_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	#major = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { province_group = kharunyana_spirit_area }
				add_devastation = 30
				add_base_tax = -1
				add_base_production = -2
				add_base_manpower = -2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.1002.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						region = shamakhad_region
						region = xianjie_region
						region = dhujat_region
						region = rahen_coast_region
					}
				}
				OR = {
					religion = high_philosophy
					religion = suhans_praxis
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -1
		custom_tooltip = kharunyana_makes_waves_tt
	}
	option = {
		name = spirits.1002.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		trigger = {
			culture = eagle_command
			AND = {
				religion = eagle_worship
				NOT = { religion = mystic_accord }
			}
		}

		change_religion = mystic_accord
		add_stability = -4
		
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = rending_ward_flag
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = rending_medium_global
				duration = -1
			}
			set_country_flag = rending_appease_flag
			set_country_flag = appeasement_in_progress
			set_country_flag = kharunyana_appeasement
			set_country_flag = kharunyana_primary
			remove_country_modifier = rending_severe_global
		}
		custom_tooltip = kharunyana_makes_waves_tt
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.1002.c
		highlight = yes
		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
		trigger = {
			culture = eagle_command
			AND = {
				religion = eagle_worship
				NOT = { religion = mystic_accord }
			}
		}
		add_stability = 1
		custom_tooltip = kharunyana_makes_waves_tt
	}

	option = {
		name = spirits.1002.d
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						culture = eagle_command
						AND = {
							religion = eagle_worship
							NOT = { religion = mystic_accord }
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						capital_scope = {
							OR = {
								region = shamakhad_region
								region = xianjie_region
								region = dhujat_region
								region = rahen_coast_region
							}
						}
						OR = {
							religion = high_philosophy
							religion = suhans_praxis
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_prestige = -1
		custom_tooltip = kharunyana_makes_waves_tt
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						4533 = {
							has_great_project = {
								type = godswall_tunnel
							}
						}
					}
				}
#				set_global_flag = rending_happened
				4533 = {
					add_great_project = {
						type = godswall_tunnel
						instant = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
